(_( Received_VBN for_IN publication_NN on_IN 7th_CD October_NNP 1936_CD )_) (_( With_IN Plates_NNP I-VI_NNP )_) INTRODUCTION_VBZ THE_DT size_NN ,_, shape_NN and_CC number_NN of_IN fat_JJ globules_NNS of_IN milk_NN are_VBP of_IN practical_JJ importance_NN in_IN the_DT separation_NN of_IN milk_NN ,_, the_DT churning_NN of_IN cream_NN ,_, the_DT shipping_NN of_IN milk_NN or_CC cream_NN over_IN long_JJ distances_NNS ,_, in_IN cheese-making_NN and_CC in_IN the_DT manufacture_NN of_IN other_JJ products_NNS of_IN milk_NN ._.
The_DT size_NN of_IN fat_JJ globules_NNS bears_VBZ a_DT relationship_NN to_TO the_DT churning_NN of_IN cream_NN as_IN the_DT cream_NN with_IN larger_JJR fat_NN globules_NNS churns_VBZ with_IN less_JJR agitation_NN than_IN that_DT in_IN which_WDT the_DT smaller_JJR globules_NNS predominate_VBP ._.
The_DT size_NN is_VBZ of_IN further_JJ importance_NN in_IN connection_NN with_IN the_DT handling_NN and_CC shipping_NN of_IN milk_NN ._.

Most_JJS of_IN the_DT Western_JJ breeds_NNS of_IN cattle_NNS have_VBP been_VBN studied_VBN and_CC classified_VBN according_VBG to_TO the_DT suitability_NN of_IN their_PRP$ milk_NN for_IN different_JJ dairy_NN products_NNS like_IN butter_NN ,_, cheese_NN ,_, milk_NN ,_, etc._FW ,_, depending_VBG on_IN the_DT size_NN ,_, shape_NN and_CC number_NN of_IN fat_JJ globules_NNS in_IN it_PRP ._.
For_IN example_NN ,_, the_DT Channel_NNP Island_NNP breeds_NNS ,_, (_( e.g._UH ,_, the_DT Jersey_NNP and_CC the_DT Guernsey_NNP )_) are_VBP known_VBN as_IN ``_`` butter_NN breeds_VBZ ``_`` due_JJ to_TO the_DT fact_NN that_IN besides_VBZ containing_VBG a_DT higher_JJR percentage_NN of_IN fat_JJ their_PRP$ milk_NN contains_VBZ fat_JJ globules_NNS of_IN large_JJ size_NN ,_, which_WDT makes_VBZ them_PRP very_RB suitable_JJ for_IN easy_JJ churning_NN and_CC consequently_RB for_IN butter-making_NN ._.
Similarly_RB of_IN all_PDT the_DT British_JJ breeds_NNS the_DT Short_NNP Horn_NNP and_CC the_DT Ayrshire_NNP are_VBP considered_VBN more_RBR suitable_JJ for_IN cheese-making_NN because_IN of_IN their_PRP$ milk_NN having_VBG fat_JJ globules_NNS of_IN medium_NN size_NN and_CC fairly_RB uniform_JJ in_IN shape_NN ._.
